93:["$","p",null,{"children":["What Bernstein and Vazirani did after showing that the Deutsch-Jozsa algorithm solves the Bernstein-Vazirani problem (as it is stated above) was to define a much more complicated problem, known as the ",["$","em",null,{"children":"recursive Fourier sampling problem"}],".\nThis is a highly contrived problem where solutions to different instances of the problem effectively unlock new levels of the problem arranged in a tree-like structure.\nThe Bernstein-Vazirani problem is essentially just the base case of this more complicated problem."],"className":"group paragraph-el text-text-primary mx-0"}]
